DBANG RGYAL GYI MA, DPON MO PHUN TSOGS DPAL 'DZOM SHU BCAS, DGA'
LDAN RAB 'BYAMS PA'I TSA BO RAB BRTAN, AER KHE JI NONG GI BLA MA
DGE 'DUN BSAM GRUB, MER GAN JI

NONG GI DPON MO BU BCAS, STAG LUNG LHUN GRUB RDZONG PA YAB YUM
SRAS BCAS KYI NGO MTSOR BYIN RLABS DANG DMANGS BRGYA SKOR LA ME
TOG GTOR, SHAL DKAR CHOS SDE'I PHRA BA DGE SLONG BLO BZANG BSAM
GRUB KYIS LAM RIM GYI KHRID 'JAM DPAL

LTAS SHIG SHAR BSEL BYANG DU KARMA GU RU'I GTER SKUS GTZOS TSAN

DANG BCAS 'BUL MI CHED DU MNGAGS, RDZONG GZHIS

KHAG KHA SHAS NAS DENG RANG RING POR 'CHO THABS LA 'BUM RGYAS PA
TSAR DRUG BRGYA BDUN CU, BRGYAD STONG PA BRGYA, GZUNGS 'DUS DRUG
BRGYA RE BDUN, MTSAN BRJOD TSIGS STONG NYIS BRGYA DRUG CU, SGROL
MA CHIG 'BUM NYI KHRI DRUG STONG DGU BRGYA RE GCIG,

GDUGS DKAR SA MA GCIG DANG CHIG 'BUM LNGA KHRI DRUG STONG NYIS
BRGYA DRUG CU, SHER SNYING NYIS 'BUM NYI KHRI DRUG STONG DGU
BRGYA ZHE GCIG, CHO GZUNGS LNGA 'BUM DRUG KHRI LNGA STONG NYIS
BRGYA, S'ATZTSA KHRI, KHRO ROL GNYIS, SREG BLU BRGYA, SNGA PA'I
RIM GROR BKA' 'GYUR

BCU GCIG, SGROL MNYIS 'BUM NYI KHRI, SHAR SNYING TSIG 'BUM GSUM

NGANG NYIS 'BUM BRGYAD KHRI, BSTAN
